<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затхлый.html>за́тхлый</a> (17874)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, a variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за́дхлый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zádxlyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>дох</a>(ну́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dox(nútʹ)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тухлый.html>ту́хлый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túxlyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затхлый.html>за́тхлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zátxlyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)за́тхлее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)за́тхлей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>musty, smelling of dampness and rot</li>
<li>stale, spoiled from long storage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> conventional, rigid, resistant to change</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stale, spoiled from storage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">залежа́лый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaležályj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">conventional</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ко́сный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kósnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рутинный.html>рути́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rutínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***затыкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затыкать.html>заты́кать</a> (13988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тыка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затыкать.html>затыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stop up, to plug, to cork
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затыкать.html>затыка́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zatykátʹ dyry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fill in holes, close gaps</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затыкать.html>затыка́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zatykátʹ rot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to silence, stop someone's mouth, stop blabbing, shut up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stick, to thrust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zatknútʹ za pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be one too many, to go one better than</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">затыкание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatykanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бочке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затычка.html>заты́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsjákoj bočke zatýčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one who has a finger in every pie</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***затягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a> (9217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">затяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корсет.html>корсе́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjágivatʹ</b> korsét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lace/tighten up a corset/girdle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjágivatʹ</b> gájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten the screws <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjágivatʹ</b> pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten one's belt; to take one's belt in</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ránu <b>zatjanúlo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wound is beginning to heal; the wound has skinned over [has closed]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to procrastinate, to delay, to drag out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjágivatʹ</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drag out a business</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфликт.html>конфли́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjágivatʹ</b> konflíkt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to protract a conflict</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pull <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to drag <i>(into)</i>, to suck <i>(into)</i>, to suck <i>(down)</i>, to engulf, to swallow up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>лошаде́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>лошаде́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lošadéj <b>zatjanúlo</b> v bolóto; bolóto <b>zatjanúlo</b> lošadéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the horses were sucked down in the bog</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to swallow up, to absorb, to engross
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивает</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta kníga prósto <b>zatjágivajet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this book really absorbs one</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start singing, to begin to harp <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рую</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычный.html>обы́чную</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:любимый.html>люби́мую</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сню</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjágivatʹ</b> stáruju (svojú obýčnuju / ljubímuju) pésnju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to (begin to) harp on one's favourite tune</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затягиваться.html>затя́гиваться</a> (8754)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягиваться.html>затя́гиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatjágivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуться.html>затяну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be tightened, to jam</li>
<li>to grow overcast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to skin over, to heal <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of wounds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затягиваться.html>затя́гивалась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rána <b>zatjágivalasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wound <b>was skinning over</b> / the wound <b>was closing</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be delayed, to be dragged out</li>
<li>to inhale (cigarette, cigar, smoking pipe)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">затяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затяжка.html>затя́жка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatjážka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затяжка.html>затя́жки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затяжка.html>затя́жки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затяжка.html>затя́жек</a></b>)
</p>

***затянуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a> (6451)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корсет.html>корсе́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zatjágivatʹ korsét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lace/tighten up a corset/girdle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjanútʹ</b> gájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten the screws <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjanútʹ</b> pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten one's belt; to take one's belt in</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ránu <b>zatjanúlo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wound is beginning to heal; the wound has skinned over [has closed]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to procrastinate, to delay, to drag out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjanútʹ</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drag out a business</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфликт.html>конфли́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjanútʹ</b> konflíkt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to protract a conflict</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pull <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to drag <i>(into)</i>, to suck <i>(into)</i>, to suck <i>(down)</i>, to engulf, to swallow up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>лошаде́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>лошаде́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lošadéj <b>zatjanúlo</b> v bolóto; bolóto <b>zatjanúlo</b> lošadéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the horses were sucked down in the bog</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to swallow up, to absorb, to engross
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta kníga prósto <b>zatjanúla</b> menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this book really absorbed me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start singing, to begin to harp <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рую</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычный.html>обы́чную</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:любимый.html>люби́мую</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сню</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatjanútʹ</b> stáruju (svojú obýčnuju / ljubímuju) pésnju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to (begin to) harp on one's favourite tune</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***затянуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затянуться.html>затяну́ться</a> (4753)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуться.html>затяну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatjanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягиваться.html>затя́гиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be tightened, to jam</li>
<li>to grow overcast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to skin over, to heal <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of wounds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуться.html>затяну́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rána <b>zatjanúlasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wound <b>has skinned over</b> / the wound <b>has closed</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be delayed, to be dragged out</li>
<li>to inhale (cigarette, cigar, smoking pipe)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затянуть.html>затяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заурядный.html>зауря́дный</a> (11227)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядовой.html>рядово́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjadovój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">average, ordinary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заурядный.html>зауря́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaurjádnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ordinary, commonplace, mediocre
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заурядный.html>зауря́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaurjádnyj</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ordinary person; a mediocrity</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зафиксировать.html>зафикси́ровать</a> (6800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fiksírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зафиксировать.html>зафикси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zafiksírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fix, to set, to settle, to state</li>
<li>to record</li>
<li>to fix <i>(a photograph)</i></li></ol>

Зализняка — 2a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захват.html>захва́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxvát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захват.html>захва́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захват.html>захва́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захват.html>захва́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>seizure, capture, taking, take, takeover</li>
<li>usurpation</li>
<li>pincher</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clench, clinch, clutch, hold</li></ol>

***захватить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a> (1721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxvatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватывать.html>захва́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grasp, to grip, to grab, to clench, to collar</li>
<li>to seize, to capture, to occupy, to usurp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:злобный.html>зло́бные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пришелец.html>прише́льцы</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zémlju <b>zaxvatíli</b> zlóbnyje prišélʹcy — ljúdi!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Earth is <b>occupied</b> by evil aliens - humans!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to absorb, to captivate, to possess, to carry away, to thrill, to engross, to enthral</li>
<li>to catch, to snatch, to take (away)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:врасплох.html>враспло́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaxvatítʹ</b> vrasplóx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch unawares, to surprise, to take by surprise</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождя́</a>.</b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Zaxvatí zont na slúčaj doždjá.</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Take</b> a brolly <b>with you</b> in case of rain.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захватчик.html>захва́тчик</a> (17715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватчик.html>захва́тчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxvátčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватчик.html>захва́тчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватчик.html>захва́тчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватчик.html>захва́тчиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">захва́тчица</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>invader, aggressor, occupier; usurper</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хва́т<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чик</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-хват-</b>; суффикс: <b>-чик</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***захватывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:захватывать.html>захва́тывать</a> (6107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватывать.html>захва́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaxvátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grasp, to grip, to grab, to clench, to collar</li>
<li>to seize, to capture, to occupy, to usurp</li>
<li>to absorb, to captivate, to possess, to carry away, to thrill, to engross, to enthral</li>
<li>to catch, to snatch, to take (away)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождя́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Zaxvatí</b> zont na slúčaj doždjá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Grab</b> an umbrella in case of a rain.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:захватить.html>захвати́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-хват-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ыва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

<p><b>зах<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ю<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>щий</b>

Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-хват-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ыва-ющ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b>.
